- `WebSocketKernel::new` no longer takes a `Vec<WebSocketRouteRegistrar>`; registered channels are built once during `AppBuilder::bootstrap()` and resolved from the DI container. Direct callers of `WebSocketKernel::new` must drop the routes argument.
- `RuntimeDiagnostics` inbound-message recording at the kernel now runs after `serde_json::from_str` parses the client message (so only parseable messages are counted). Malformed frames no longer increment `inbound_messages_total`.
- WebSocket wire actions are documented as canonical `snake_case`; legacy PascalCase action aliases remain accepted for compatibility.
- WebSocket room routing is now explicit: channel-wide publishes reach all subscribers, while room publishes reach only exact room subscribers.
- WebSocket `on_leave` hooks and `presence:leave` now run for unsubscribe, socket close, heartbeat timeout, and force disconnect.
- WebSocket channel callbacks now receive owned context/channel/room values, which makes async closures easier to use safely.

### Breaking

- `EmailMessage::template(...)` is now `async` (template files are read off the async runtime); add `.await` before the `?`.
- TOTP MFA switched from HMAC-SHA256 to RFC 6238 HMAC-SHA1 (see Security); previously enrolled TOTP factors must be re-enrolled.
- Validation: `min_numeric`, `max_numeric`, `between`, and `numeric` are stricter (see Security); requests that previously passed with non-numeric values in bounded fields now fail validation.
- `#[derive(Validate)]` no longer auto-skips rules for `Option<T>` fields that explicitly include `required`; missing/empty values now fail `required`. Consumer follow-up: remove `required` or add explicit `nullable` when absence is intended to be valid.
- Derived multipart extractors now reject missing non-`Option` text fields with `400 Bad Request` instead of constructing `Default::default()`. Consumer follow-up: send every non-optional multipart field, or model intentionally omitted fields as `Option<T>`/`Vec<T>`.
- `#[derive(ApiSchema)]` now rejects `#[serde(flatten)]` on `Option<T>` fields at compile time because Foundry's TypeScript exporter cannot represent optional flattened structs safely. Consumer follow-up: flatten a normal child DTO and put `Option` on each child field that may be omitted.
- `#[derive(ApiSchema)]` and `#[derive(Validate)]` now reject `#[serde(deny_unknown_fields)]` DTOs that also contain `#[serde(flatten)]` fields because serde cannot safely combine flattened fields with strict unknown-field rejection. Consumer follow-up: remove `deny_unknown_fields`, replace the flattened child with explicit fields, or split the strict request DTO from the flattened serialization DTO.
- `#[derive(Validate)]` now rejects `#[serde(flatten)]` fields that also carry `#[validate(...)]` rules because validation error paths and generated TypeScript metadata cannot safely target flattened JSON keys yet. Consumer follow-up: move validation rules to explicit parent fields, validate the child DTO outside flattening, or avoid flattening DTOs that need nested validation.
- `#[derive(ApiSchema)]` and `#[derive(foundry::TS)]` now reject non-`Option` `#[serde(default)]` fields unless they also use `#[ts(optional, as = "Option<_>")]` or `#[validate(required)]`, and reject `#[serde(skip_serializing_if = "...")]` fields unless they use `#[ts(optional)]`. Consumer follow-up: add the TS optional annotation when omission is valid, or add `required` validation when clients must still send a defaulted request field.
- `#[derive(ApiSchema)]` and `#[derive(foundry::TS)]` now reject directional serde skips (`#[serde(skip_serializing)]` / `#[serde(skip_deserializing)]`) because one generated TypeScript/OpenAPI contract cannot represent different request and response field sets, and `ts-rs` ignores those attributes. Consumer follow-up: split request and response DTOs for directional fields, or use `#[serde(skip)]` / `#[ts(skip)]` when a field is never part of the public contract.
- Derived OpenAPI schemas now honor `#[serde(deny_unknown_fields)]` by emitting `additionalProperties: false`, matching serde's runtime rejection of extra object fields. Consumer follow-up: regenerate OpenAPI docs/clients if DTOs use `deny_unknown_fields`; schema-driven clients may now reject extra fields earlier instead of relying on backend validation.
- Derived TypeScript validation metadata now honors `#[serde(deny_unknown_fields)]` by emitting `denyUnknownFields: true` plus a full `knownFields` request shape, and the generated route-helper runtime reports extra request keys as `unknown_field` validation errors. Manual validators can opt in with `.deny_unknown_fields().known_fields([...])`. Consumer follow-up: regenerate frontend types/helpers if strict DTOs derive `Validate`; direct `TsValidationSchema { ... }` literals must set `deny_unknown_fields: false` and `known_fields: Vec::new()`, or switch to `TsValidationSchema::new()`.
- WebSocket `message` and `client_event` frames now require an active matching channel/room subscription before handlers or client-event relay run.
